00095 /* YYLLOC_DEFAULT -- Set CURRENT to span from RHS[1] to RHS[N].
00096    If N is 0, then set CURRENT to the empty location which ends
00097    the previous symbol: RHS[0] (always defined).  */
00098 
00099 #define YYRHSLOC(Rhs, K) ((Rhs)[K])
00100 #ifndef YYLLOC_DEFAULT
00101 # define YYLLOC_DEFAULT(Current, Rhs, N)                               \
00102  do                                                                    \
00103    if (N)                                                              \
00104      {                                                                 \
00105        (Current).begin = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, 1).begin;                      \
00106        (Current).end   = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, N).end;                        \
00107      }                                                                 \
00108    else                                                                \
00109      {                                                                 \
00110        (Current).begin = (Current).end = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, 0).end;        \
00111      }                                                                 \
00112  while (false)
00113 #endif

00169   /* Return YYSTR after stripping away unnecessary quotes and
00170      backslashes, so that it's suitable for yyerror.  The heuristic is
00171      that double-quoting is unnecessary unless the string contains an
00172      apostrophe, a comma, or backslash (other than backslash-backslash).
00173      YYSTR is taken from yytname.  */
00174   std::string
00175   ParserImplementation::yytnamerr_ (const char *yystr)
00176   {
00177     if (*yystr == '"')
00178       {
00179         std::string yyr = "";
00180         char const *yyp = yystr;
00181 
00182         for (;;)
00183           switch (*++yyp)
00184             {
00185             case '\'':
00186             case ',':
00187               goto do_not_strip_quotes;
00188 
00189             case '\\':
00190               if (*++yyp != '\\')
00191                 goto do_not_strip_quotes;
00192               /* Fall through.  */
00193             default:
00194               yyr += *yyp;
00195               break;
00196 
00197             case '"':
00198               return yyr;
00199             }
00200       do_not_strip_quotes: ;
00201       }
00202 
00203     return yystr;
00204   }

04494   yyerrlab1:
04495     yyerrstatus_ = 3;   /* Each real token shifted decrements this.  */
04496 
04497     for (;;)

04499         yyn = yypact_[yystate];
04500         if (!yy_pact_value_is_default_ (yyn))
04501         {
04502           yyn += yyterror_;
04503           if (0 <= yyn && yyn <= yylast_ && yycheck_[yyn] == yyterror_)
04504             {
04505               yyn = yytable_[yyn];
04506               if (0 < yyn)
04507                 break;
04508             }
04509         }
04510 
04511         /* Pop the current state because it cannot handle the error token.  */
04512         if (yystate_stack_.height () == 1)

04544   yyabortlab:

04559        this YYABORT or YYACCEPT.  */
04560     yypop_ (yylen);

04564                    yystos_[yystate_stack_[0]],
04565                    &yysemantic_stack_[0],
04566                    &yylocation_stack_[0]);
04567         yypop_ ();

04569 
04570     return yyresult;
04571   }

04573   // Generate an error message.
04574   std::string
04575   ParserImplementation::yysyntax_error_ (int yystate, int yytoken)
04576   {
04577     std::string yyres;
04578     // Number of reported tokens (one for the "unexpected", one per
04579     // "expected").
04580     size_t yycount = 0;
04581     // Its maximum.
04582     enum { YYERROR_VERBOSE_ARGS_MAXIMUM = 5 };
04583     // Arguments of yyformat.
04584     char const *yyarg[YYERROR_VERBOSE_ARGS_MAXIMUM];
04585 
04586     /* There are many possibilities here to consider:
04587        - If this state is a consistent state with a default action, then
04588          the only way this function was invoked is if the default action
04589          is an error action.  In that case, don't check for expected
04590          tokens because there are none.
04591        - The only way there can be no lookahead present (in yytoken) is
04592          if this state is a consistent state with a default action.
04593          Thus, detecting the absence of a lookahead is sufficient to
04594          determine that there is no unexpected or expected token to
04595          report.  In that case, just report a simple "syntax error".
04596        - Don't assume there isn't a lookahead just because this state is
04597          a consistent state with a default action.  There might have
04598          been a previous inconsistent state, consistent state with a
04599          non-default action, or user semantic action that manipulated
04600          yychar.
04601        - Of course, the expected token list depends on states to have
04602          correct lookahead information, and it depends on the parser not
04603          to perform extra reductions after fetching a lookahead from the
04604          scanner and before detecting a syntax error.  Thus, state
04605          merging (from LALR or IELR) and default reductions corrupt the
04606          expected token list.  However, the list is correct for
04607          canonical LR with one exception: it will still contain any
04608          token that will not be accepted due to an error action in a
04609          later state.
04610     */
04611     if (yytoken != yyempty_)
04612       {
04613         yyarg[yycount++] = yytname_[yytoken];
04614         int yyn = yypact_[yystate];
04615         if (!yy_pact_value_is_default_ (yyn))
04616           {
04617             /* Start YYX at -YYN if negative to avoid negative indexes in
04618                YYCHECK.  In other words, skip the first -YYN actions for
04619                this state because they are default actions.  */
04620             int yyxbegin = yyn < 0 ? -yyn : 0;
04621             /* Stay within bounds of both yycheck and yytname.  */
04622             int yychecklim = yylast_ - yyn + 1;
04623             int yyxend = yychecklim < yyntokens_ ? yychecklim : yyntokens_;
04624             for (int yyx = yyxbegin; yyx < yyxend; ++yyx)
04625               if (yycheck_[yyx + yyn] == yyx && yyx != yyterror_
04626                   && !yy_table_value_is_error_ (yytable_[yyx + yyn]))
04627                 {
04628                   if (yycount == YYERROR_VERBOSE_ARGS_MAXIMUM)
04629                     {
04630                       yycount = 1;
04631                       break;
04632                     }
04633                   else
04634                     yyarg[yycount++] = yytname_[yyx];
04635                 }
04636           }
04637       }
04638 
04639     char const* yyformat = 0;
04640     switch (yycount)
04641       {
04642 #define YYCASE_(N, S)                         \
04643         case N:                               \
04644           yyformat = S;                       \
04645         break
04646         YYCASE_(0, YY_("syntax error"));
04647         YYCASE_(1, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s"));
04648         YYCASE_(2, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s"));
04649         YYCASE_(3, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s"));
04650         YYCASE_(4, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s or %s"));
04651         YYCASE_(5, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s or %s or %s"));
04652 #undef YYCASE_
04653       }
04654 
04655     // Argument number.
04656     size_t yyi = 0;
04657     for (char const* yyp = yyformat; *yyp; ++yyp)
04658       if (yyp[0] == '%' && yyp[1] == 's' && yyi < yycount)
04659         {
04660           yyres += yytnamerr_ (yyarg[yyi++]);
04661           ++yyp;
04662         }
04663       else
04664         yyres += *yyp;
04665     return yyres;
04666   }

06079   // Report on the debug stream that the rule \a yyrule is going to be reduced.
06080   void
06081   ParserImplementation::yy_reduce_print_ (int yyrule)
06082   {
06083     unsigned int yylno = yyrline_[yyrule];
06084     int yynrhs = yyr2_[yyrule];
06085     /* Print the symbols being reduced, and their result.  */
06086     *yycdebug_ << "Reducing stack by rule " << yyrule - 1
06087                << " (line " << yylno << "):" << std::endl;
06088     /* The symbols being reduced.  */
06089     for (int yyi = 0; yyi < yynrhs; yyi++)
06090       YY_SYMBOL_PRINT ("   $" << yyi + 1 << " =",
06091                        yyrhs_[yyprhs_[yyrule] + yyi],
06092                        &(yysemantic_stack_[(yynrhs) - (yyi + 1)]),
06093                        &(yylocation_stack_[(yynrhs) - (yyi + 1)]));
06094   }
06095 #endif // YYDEBUG

06173 
06174 void Replace( std::string& msg , const char* find , const char* rep ) {
06175   size_t pos = 0;
06176   while ( ( pos = msg.find( find , 0 ) ) != std::string::npos ) {
06177     msg.replace( pos , strlen( find ) , rep );
06178   }
06179 }
06180 
06181 void yy::ParserImplementation::error (const location_type& loc, const std::string& row_msg ) {
06182   std::string msg = row_msg;
